## 论文文本提取:
```json
{
  "有害标准": {
    "标准1": {
      "内容": "模因包含对女性的侮辱性或攻击性内容，直接表达对女性的仇恨或偏见。",
      "对应原文": "A meme is misogynous if it conceptually describes an offensive, sexist or hateful scene (weak or strong, implicitly or explicitly) having as target a woman or a group of women."
    },
    "标准2": {
      "内容": "模因涉及对女性的身体或性别特征的羞辱，例如身体羞辱或性别刻板印象。",
      "对应原文": "These types of misogynous memes are related to denigrating the physical appearance of women (body shaming)."
    },
    "标准3": {
      "内容": "模因表现出对女性的物化，视女性为物品或仅仅是身体的存在。",
      "对应原文": "It is a practice of seeing and/or treating a woman like an object."
    },
    "标准4": {
      "内容": "模因暗示或直接呼吁对女性的暴力行为。",
      "对应原文": "These types of misogynous memes are aimed at showing violence against women or at alluding to the intent of physically assert power over women."
    }
  },
  "无害标准": {
    "标准1": {
      "内容": "模因不包含任何针对女性的仇恨、偏见或攻击性内容。",
      "对应原文": "A meme is NOT misogynous if it is conceptually not related to women or even if it is related to women, but it does not represent an offensive, sexist or hateful concept against women."
    },
    "标准2": {
      "内容": "模因的内容与女性无关，或仅仅是中立的描述，没有任何贬低或攻击的意图。",
      "对应原文": "A meme that does not express any form of hate against women."
    },
    "标准3": {
      "内容": "模因可能包含幽默或讽刺的元素，但不涉及对女性的贬低或物化。",
      "对应原文": "Although many memes are created with humorous intent, others have political or activist ambitions."
    }
  }
}
```

### 错误样本ID: 3248

  "判别出错原因分析": "在当前模型对模因的评估中，打分结果明显偏离了Ground Truth（GT），将其误判为无害而实际上是有害。这一错误的主要原因在于对Harmful Scores（有害分数）的判别维度理解不足。首先，在维度H1（Targeted Entity Existence）上，模型未能充分识别该模因间接针对女性的内容。模因文本提到的'THE ONLY GIRL YOU MATCH WITH ON TINDER'，虽然表面上看似在讨论约会，但实际上暗示了对女性在社交交往中受到的物化和羞辱，这种内容属于攻击性和贬低女性的范畴。因此，H1的得分应提升。其次，在维度H2（Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Content）上，内容传达的性别歧视信息未被充分考虑，模型应针对任何对女性有攻击性或贬低性意图的内容给予更高分数。此外，H3（Multimodal Nature of Harm）受图文结合影响严重，其结果未能清晰显现图与文间的有害语境关系。总之，这些维度的得分缺乏对模因整体内容中对女性的潜在贬低的敏感性，这是导致最终错误判别的根本原因。在无害维度N1（No Targeted Entity）上，模型给予了较低评分，但未能充分理解模因的内涵与其可能产生的影响。因此，增加维度以提升现有评估对复杂内容的敏感性，将是必要的改进方向。",

        "details": "此维度主要关注模因文本中是否存在潜在的性别歧视或贬低元素，尽管表面文字可能缺乏直接攻击，但诸如约会平台的引用可能隐含了对女性的物化或假设。评估者应分析文本背后的社会文化语境，判断其是否反映出对女性的不平等期待或评价。此维度的引入将增加对模因复杂性和深层意义的理解，从而提高判别的准确性。"

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因ID: 5718和ID: 3248的错误分析中，专家们提出了一系列关于如何改进模因有害性判别的看法。经过综合分析，我们提出了两条主要的操作建议，以提升对模因中性别歧视内容的敏感性和准确性。

首先，我们建议**新增两个维度**。第一个是“**女性物化的维度（Dimensional Reflection of Objectification）**”，该维度旨在强调模因中女性被物化的现象。当模因描绘女性为物体或满足特定审美标准的存在时，这种情况应当被单独评估。通过引入此维度，可以更全面地评估模因的有害性，特别是在认知女性的社会身份方面。第二个新增的维度是“**幽默内容的背景分析（Contextual Humor Analysis）**”，该维度将单独评估幽默元素对女性的潜在攻击性。这一分析将有助于深入理解幽默是否淡化了性别问题，或是依然带有物化与贬低的意味，从而提升误判的敏感性。

其次，我们将**删除与合并现有维度**。由于模因的性质发生了变化，H1维度（Targeted Entity Existence）表现异常，被判定为漏报，建议删除该维度，以便于合理评估模因对女性的直接攻击意图。而N2维度（Harmless Scores）打分过高，应删除该维度，以清晰反映模因的真正潜在有害性。此外，我们将H和N维度的数量调整至4个，保持整体评估的精简与有效。

最后，在评估打分时，我们特别强调应避免将H得分压制在高分，而N得分则偏低的极端情况。每个维度分数应独立进行，并应充分考虑模因中隐含的性别歧视信息，以保证判别的准确性和公正性。这种改进方案聚焦于提升模因评估模型对复杂社交与文化语境的敏感性，旨在为后续的模因判别过程提供更科学、更具参考价值的依据。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator tasked with scoring a meme based on the MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your objective is not to label the meme as 'misogynous' or 'not misogynous,' but to assign scores from 1 to 9 for each dimension, wherein 1 indicates complete absence and 9 denotes full presence.

**Critical Instructions Before Scoring:**

1. **Definition Clarity**  
   - **Harmful Content (Misogynous)**: A meme is deemed harmful if it contains offensive, sexist, or hateful elements directed at women, either implicitly or explicitly.  
   - **Harmless Content (Not Misogynous)**: A meme may be classified as harmless if it does not convey hate against women—either by being unrelated to them or involving them without discriminatory content.

2. **Harm Representation**  
   - Evaluate if harm is presented **implicitly** (e.g., subtle visual cues) or **explicitly** (e.g., direct hate speech). Both forms need to be considered for harmful scoring.

3. **Image-Text Dynamics**  
   - Determine if the offensive meaning arises only through the combination of image and text, both of which must be evaluated together as per MAMI principles.

4. **Contextual Evaluation**  
   - Consider the following queries:
     - "Can this be reasonably interpreted as offensive or hateful toward women?"
     - "Does the meme present negative content about women as a fact or as absurd humor without real-world harm?"
     - "Does it critique gender norms without derogatory framing of women?" If it does, consider it harmless.

**Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria (Misogynous):**
- **H1: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
  Score high if the meme targets women with offensive or sexist implications. This encompasses explicit and implicit content aimed at women.

- **H2: Objectification of Women**  
  Score high if the meme depicts women as objects or adheres to specific beauty standards, undermining their social identity.

- **H3: Humor's Contextual Analysis**  
  Score high if the humorous elements are derogatory or imply objectification, which necessitates scrutiny of how humor is positioned within the content.

- **H4: Multimodal Assessment**  
  Score high if harmful perceptions arise from the interplay of image and text working in tandem, as mandated by MAMI's multi-modal framework.

**Harmless Criteria (Not Misogynous):**
- **N1: Absence of Targeted Entity**  
  Score high only if no identifiable woman or female group is depicted in a derogatory manner.

- **N2: Filtering Conditions Adherence**  
  Score high if it meets criteria such as being non-English, unreadable, or merely a single modality (text-only or image-only) without meaningful interaction.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
  Score high if:
    - The content is entirely fantastical without features that represent women negatively, or
    - It critiques societal structures without implicating real women in derogatory contexts. If a real woman is portrayed and labeled derogatorily, assign N3 a score of 3 or below. If depicted in a fictional or fantastical light without such implications, N3 can score 6 or higher.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a concise justification based on MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme includes offensive or sexist elements targeting women (implicit/explicit), (2) whether the harm is dependent on the interaction of image and text, and (3) the rationale for the N3 score based on derogatory content or fantastical context."
}

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在近年来对模因的有害性判别中，专家提出了一系列建设性的建议，强调了评估标准的细化和维度的完善。基于汇总的信息，我们提出了两条核心操作建议，以优化模因的判别流程和提高评分的准确性。

第一条建议是新增维度。鉴于现有评估标准对幽默元素与女性内容之间关系的分析不足，我们建议新增维度“H5: Humor and Contextual Impact”。该维度将专注于评估模因中幽默是否潜在隐含性别攻击或物化倾向。具体而言，模因的幽默表达应被评估其上下文，如何影响观众对女性的态度，以及是否可能建立刻板印象，这是当前评分体系急需加强的方面。此外，考虑到性别物化的相关问题，我们还建议新增维度“H6: Power Dynamics”。该维度将帮助分析模因如何反映和加强现有的性别权力结构，揭示模因在叙事中对权力关系的表现及其对观众潜在影响的理解。

第二条建议是重写现有维度，对“Harmful Scores”中的H1（Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent）和H2（Objectification of Women）进行调整，以更加准确地反映模因中的贬低意图。评估人员需要增强对视觉与文本结合所产生的影响的重视，确保能有效捕捉到模因通过饱含贬低或物化女性的信息，从而导致的潜在伤害。此外，现有的Harmless Scores中N1的分数调整也应工具化，确保不被误解为模因中对女性的表现是无害的。

通过实施这两条建议，可以更全面地捕捉模因对女性的影响，从而确保评分体系更具准确性和可靠性。最终的目标是建立一个更为合理和有效的评估标准，使得对模因的判别可以在性别敏感性方面深入人心。


---

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are assigned the critical role of evaluating a meme according to the MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your primary goal is to provide scores from 1 to 9 across various dimensions, where a score of 1 signifies the complete absence of harmful elements and a score of 9 reflects their full presence.

**Essential Instructions Before Scoring:**

1. **Clarify Definitions**  
   - **Harmful Content**: A meme is classified as harmful if it contains offensive, sexist, or hateful elements directed toward women, either in explicit language or subtle insinuations.  
   - **Harmless Content**: Assign a harmless classification if the meme does not target women with hatred, whether by being entirely unrelated or depicting them without discrimination.

2. **Analysis of Harm**  
   - Assess harm from both **implicitly** (e.g., subtle cues or visuals) and **explicitly** (e.g., overt hate speech) conveyed messages. Ensure nuanced understanding is applied when scoring harmful content.

3. **Interaction of Elements**  
   - Evaluate whether the offensive meaning emerges solely from a combination of image and text. It is imperative to consider how these elements interact as per MAMI’s principles.

4. **Contextual Evaluation**  
   - Reflect on the following questions during evaluation:
     - "Can this meme be interpreted as offensive or hateful towards women?"
     - "Is the negative portrayal of women presented as fact or absurd humor without real-world implications?"
     - "Does the content critique gender norms without derogatory implications for women?" If so, classify it as harmless.

**Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria:**
- **H1: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
  Score highly if the meme explicitly or implicitly conveys offensive, sexist taunts directed at women. Focus on the combination of visual and textual elements that may convey this intent.

- **H2: Objectification of Women**  
  Score highly if the meme portrays women as objects, reinforcing stereotypes or specific beauty standards.

- **H3: Humor's Contextual Analysis**  
  Score highly if humor is derogatory or suggests objectification, demanding careful evaluation of how humor influences perceptions of women.

- **H4: Multimodal Assessment**  
  Score high if harmful interpretations arise from the complementarity of image and text, emphasizing the need for holistic evaluation.

- **H5: Humor and Contextual Impact**  
  Score high based on whether humor reveals underlying gender attacks or objectification, examining the broader societal implications of the meme.

- **H6: Power Dynamics**  
  Score high if the meme reflects or reinforces existing gender power structures, analyzing how power relations are depicted and their potential influence on the audience.

**Harmless Criteria:**
- **N1: Absence of Targeted Entity**  
  Score highly if no identifiable women or female groups appear in a derogatory manner, ensuring clarity in depiction.

- **N2: Filtering Conditions Adherence**  
  Score highly if it qualifies by being non-English, unreadable, or single-modality (text-only or image-only), devoid of meaningful interaction.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
  Score high if:
    - Content is outrightly fantastical with no negative representations of women, or
    - It critiques societal structures without portraying real women offensively. If a real woman is depicted derogatorily, N3 should score 3 or lower; in a fantastical context without such implications, a score of 6 or higher may apply.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int
  },

### 错误样本ID: 9416
**错误原因分析:** {
  "判别出错原因分析": "在对模因的有害性和无害性的评估中，当前分数出错的主要原因在于对内容的解读和维度打分的微妙差别。根据GT，这一模因被认定为有害，而模型的打分则表现出了对无害性更高的偏向，导致错误的分类。一方面，'H1'维度的评分较低（3分）未能反映出模因中可能包含的隐含性别偏见或贬低成分，尤其是在对女性形象的比较上，左侧的老照片与右侧现代女性的对比实际上暗示了不同世代对女性身体和美的期望，可能并不完全中立。'H2'维度的评分（2分）同样不足以体现物化的潜在表现，尤其是对比两种穿着风格的表达可能会引导观众将女性视为物件的一种表现。'N1'的评分为6分，显示出模型认为模因中存在中立内容，这与GT相悖，因为模因的对比本身包含了针对女性的暗示性评判，导致其抗拒将其标识为有害内容。因此，存在评估引导不够明确且缺乏对多模态交互理解的情况，必须增强这一层面的评分能力，使其反映复杂的文化语境。","满足修正决策的维度集合以及需要采取的操作": {
    "需要新增维度": {
      "H5": {
        "action": "新增",
        "reason": "模因的审视需要多模态的交织影响，H5维度将针对模因中性别表现及其文化语境进行更深入的探讨。具体来说，H5将考虑内容所传达的性别期望与刻板印象，帮助评估是否有不当的性别暗示和对象化的内容，因此该维度可以更准确地捕捉到模因对女性形象的影响。这种文化层面的分析对正确评判有害内容至关重要，在当前的评估系统中缺乏这一维度的关注可能导致误判。此外，通过引入集中的性别文化分析维度，可以更准确地衡量模因背后潜在的性别偏见，因此对于理解当前模因中隐性及显性对女性态度有重要作用。",
        "details": "该维度专注于分析模因所构建的性别期望和社会性别角色的表现，包括分析模因中展示的女性形象是否强化了特定的性别刻板印象，是否存在贬低其社会身份的隐性内容。评估该维度时将针对具体的模因内容，检查其是否在隐含地暗示着女性的价值只依赖于外貌或表现，而忽略其独立个体性。此外，该维度还会考虑到模因使用的社会文化背景，以判断其可能对社会性别观念产生的影响。"

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在专家的对模因有害性和无害性的评估建议中，两个模因（9416和8102）均存在分类错误的情况，主要是由于对内容的解读和维度打分的微妙差别。在这两个案例中，模因的性别偏见及其文化语境没有受到充分考虑，导致模型对于有害内容的敏感度不足。

首先，建议新增H5维度，专注分析模因中性别表现及其文化语境。这一维度将深入探讨模因所传达的性别期望与刻板印象，对女性身份的物化和贬低可能的隐性内容进行更细致的评估。H5的引入将有效填补当前系统对复杂文化语境理解的缺口，确保模因对女性的影响能够得到准确衡量。

其次，建议新增两个维度来提升对模因的评估能力。第一个是专门评估幽默元素潜在攻击性的维度，该维度将帮助识别幽默内容是否在表面上是玩笑，却又暗藏对女性的嘲讽与轻视。幽默可能有助于掩盖深层的歧视，因此需要更为细致的考量。第二个维度则关注图像与文本的互动，分析其如何共同传达有害信息。这种交互的审视将帮助提升对模因内容的精准判断，使其在传递的语义上更加全面。

总体而言，通过新增H5、幽默攻击性评估和图文互动评估这三个维度，将有效提高对模因有害性和无害性的判别能力，避免当前评估系统在处理复杂内容时的误判。同时，消除对H1、H2等维度的不足表现，保持H和N维度在3-7之间，确保系统的评估机制更加有效和灵活。这样的改进将为理解模因及其潜在影响提供更为准确的依据，有助于保护社会文化的健康与多元。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator tasked with systematically scoring a meme according to the refined MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your goal is to assign scores ranging from 1 to 9 for each defined dimension, where 1 indicates no presence and 9 indicates complete presence of the assessed criterion.

**Critical Instructions Before Scoring:**

1. **Definition Clarity**  
   - **Harmful Content (Misogynous)**: Classify a meme as harmful if it expresses discriminatory, offensive, or hateful sentiments directed at women, whether these elements are overt or subtly implied.  
   - **Harmless Content (Not Misogynous)**: A meme can be deemed harmless if it features women in a neutral or positive manner, or if it involves them in a creative or absurd context without offensive undertones.

2. **Harm Representation**  
   - Assess whether harm is depicted **explicitly** (e.g., direct derogatory language) or **implicitly** (e.g., hidden visual cues). Both contexts must be evaluated meticulously.

3. **Image-Text Interaction**  
   - Examine if the offensive meaning emerges solely from the combination of image and text, which must be analyzed together as instructed by MAMI principles.

4. **Contextual Evaluation**  
   - Reflect on these guiding questions:
     - "Is there a reasonable interpretation of the meme as offensive or derogatory towards women?"
     - "Does the meme trivialize women's issues under the guise of humor that lacks real-world harm?"
     - "Does it provide a critique of gender norms without putting women in a negative light?" If it does, categorize it as harmless.

5. **Additional Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H5: Gender Representation and Cultural Context**  
     Score high if the meme perpetuates harmful gender stereotypes or objectifies women within its cultural framework. Examine how these elements impact the perception of women's identities.

   - **H6: Humor's Potential for Offense**  
     Score high if the humor is misleadingly benign but conceals mockery or derision towards women. Humor requires careful scrutiny to uncover deeper biases.

   - **H7: Image-Text Harmful Interaction Assessment**  
     Score high when examining the synergistic interaction between image and text that conveys harmful implications, aligning with MAMI’s multimodal evaluation structure.

**Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria (Misogynous):**
- **H1: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
Score higher for memes that directly or indirectly target women with negative implications.

- **H2: Objectification of Women**  
Score high for images that convey women as objects or emphasize harmful beauty ideals that detract from their identities.

- **H3: Humor's Contextual Analysis**  
Score high for memes where humor reinforces derogatory views or objectification. Analyze the placement and implications of humor thoroughly.

- **H4: Multimodal Assessment**  
Score high if the harmful meaning emerges exclusively through the interplay between image and text.

**Harmless Criteria (Not Misogynous):**
- **N1: Absence of Targeted Entity**  
Score high when no identifiable individuals or groups of women are portrayed negatively.

- **N2: Filtering Conditions Adherence**  
Score high for memes that are non-English, non-readable, or presented in a single modality (whether text or image) without meaningful interactivity.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
Score high if:
  - The content is entirely fantastical with no negative representations of women, or
  - It critiques societal norms without involving real women derogatorily. If a real woman is derogatorily labeled, limit N3 to a score of 3 or below; in fantasy depictions devoid of such implications, N3 can score 6 or higher.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int,
    "H7": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a succinct justification based on MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme includes offensive or sexist elements targeting women (implicit/explicit), (2) whether the harm classification relies on the relationship of image and text, (3) the rationale for the N3 score based on derogatory content or fantastical elements."
}

The representation of women in beauty pageants can perpetuate harmful stereotypes (H5: 4). The humor, while seemingly benign, can be seen as mocking the outrage itself (H6: 5). The interaction between the image and text suggests a critique that may not fully escape the objectifying context (H7: 5). For harmless criteria, the meme does depict a woman but does not target her negatively in a direct manner (N1: 2). The meme is in English and readable (N2: 1). The content critiques societal norms but does so through a lens that still involves real women in a potentially derogatory context (N3: 4)."
}

## pre1l0记忆更新
**输出:**
审视模因9973的判别出错原因，专家们建议从多个维度进行修正，以提高对模因幽默性与潜在冒犯性的判别精准度。首先，我们应新增两个维度，以涵盖幽默及荒诞内容的独特处理方式，这些内容在社交文化中常通过讽刺与夸张表达，影响观众的理解方向。

第一，新增“幽默解析”维度，该维度专注于评估模因中幽默的种类与表达方式。评审时，需考虑幽默的意图是否具创造性，以及其在社会文化中的作用。这有助于评审者识别出幽默是否是善意的调侃，而非简单的冒犯，使得对含有幽默的模因的评估更为准确，避免误判。

第二，新增“荒诞处理”维度，它要求评审者从超现实与讽刺的角度分析内容，着重判断模因是否采用荒诞的表现手法。在许多情况下，模因看似冒犯的内容可能实际上是在日常幽默文化中与荒诞场景相结合的结果。因此，通过此维度，评审者将能更好地理解模因的风格与文化背景，优化其最终打分结果。

与此同时，鉴于目前打分偏向极端，我们建议调整“H”和“N”维度的整体数量，以确保评分体系的平衡和客观性。例如，“N2”维度虽能识别部分无害性，但得分较低，需通过与新增维度的整合提升其准确性。

总之，通过以上的维度创新与调整，我们旨在提升模因评估的全面性与准确性，让模因的幽默性在评判中不再被忽视，同时保障对冒犯内容的合理识别。这一过程将有助于清晰界定当今网络文化下模因的多元解读，从而在不断演进的评估体系中，形成更加准确且文化适宜的判别标准。

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因的有害性和无害性判别过程中，结合各位专家的分析，存在明显的需要进一步完善的维度以及更清晰的评估标准。为此，建议采取以下两条核心操作建议，以优化模型的评估效果。

首先，针对模因中涉及女性角色的表达，需要新增两个维度，分别为H8（女性主义讽刺评估）和N4（文化性别议题探讨）。H8维度将重点关注模因中如何通过幽默的方式处理女性主义议题，以识别其中可能存在的性别歧视暗示和幽默对女性的潜在影响。这一维度的添加将帮助评审员更深刻地理解模因的幽默性质与社会倡导信号之间的关系。N4维度则将探讨模因是否有意图在幽默中探讨性别不平等问题，帮助分析模因是否在呼吁对性别话题的理解与批判，还是仅仅强化了对某一性别的不尊重。通过这两个维度的引入，我们期待可以大幅增强对模因有害性的判别能力。

其次，需要在无害样本的维度中进行优化，特别是要针对N2（无害内容识别）进行重写，确保其更加关注模因中可能隐藏的贬低或刻板印象。将N2重新定义为“无害内容的积极构建”，要求评审员在判断模因是否真的无害时，不仅考虑表面内容的直接表述，还需从社会文化背景的层面识别潜藏的信息和影响。这一举措将有助于平衡无害性相关的评估，避免误判无害样本。

最终目标是保持评估维度的科学性和合理性，确保在H与N维度中都能够准确反映模因的真正意图与社会效果，从而提高整套模因判别体系的准确性与严谨性。通过这些针对性的更新与优化，可望提升模型在性别议题模因评估中的表现，为打击潜在的性别歧视与偏见铺平道路。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are tasked with evaluating a meme based on updated MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your objective is to assign comprehensive scores from 1 to 9 for each specified dimension, where 1 signifies no presence and 9 indicates complete presence of the assessed criterion.

**Evaluation Instructions:**

1. **Clarified Definitions**  
   - **Harmful Content (Misogynous)**: Identify a meme as harmful if it presents discriminatory, derogatory, or abusive sentiments toward women, whether they are expressed overtly or subtly concealed.  
   - **Harmless Content (Not Misogynous)**: A meme can be considered harmless if it depicts women in a neutral, positive, or humorous context that lacks offensive implications.

2. **Harm Assessment**  
   - Determine whether harm is demonstrated **explicitly** (e.g., overtly insulting language) or **implicitly** (e.g., nuanced visual cues). Both elements need careful evaluation.

3. **Image-Text Relationship**  
   - Analyze the fusion of image and text to see if harmful implications emerge only from their combination, adhering to MAMI’s multimodal principles.

4. **Contextual Analysis**  
   - Reflect on these questions:
     - "Can the meme be reasonably interpreted as offensive or derogatory toward women?"
     - "Does it trivialize women's issues in a humorless way?"
     - "Does it critique gender norms while avoiding a negative portrayal of women?" If yes, consider it harmless.

5. **Expanded Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H5: Gender Representation and Cultural Context**  
     Score higher if the meme propagates harmful gender stereotypes or objectifies women in its cultural setting, evaluating impacts on perceiving women's identities.

   - **H6: Humor's Potential for Offense**  
     Score high if the humor appears innocuous but carries underlying mockery or contempt for women. Humor warrants scrutinous analysis to reveal deeper biases.

   - **H7: Image-Text Harmful Interaction Assessment**  
     Score high when the interaction between image and text signifies harmful implications, aligning with MAMI’s multimodal evaluation.

   - **H8: Feminist Satire Evaluation**  
     Assess whether humor in the meme addresses feminist themes and identify any latent sexist implications. This dimension aims to enhance recognition of how humor interacts with social commentary.

   - **N4: Constructive Harmlessness Evaluation**  
     Redefine to assess if the meme meaningfully addresses gender issues without derogatory implications or stereotypes. Focus on potential positive representations of women.

**Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria (Misogynous):**
- **H1: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
Score higher for memes that insult, demean, or target women directly or indirectly.

- **H2: Objectification of Women**  
Score high for visuals that portray women as objects or promote harmful beauty standards detracting from their identity.

- **H3: Humor's Contextual Analysis**  
Score high where humor reinforces derogatory stereotypes; thoroughly analyze humor's implications.

- **H4: Multimodal Assessment**  
Score high if negative meanings arise solely through the interplay of image and text.

**Harmless Criteria (Not Misogynous):**
- **N1: Absence of Targeted Entity**  
Score high when no identifiable women or groups are portrayed negatively.

- **N2: Active Construct of Harmlessness**  
Score high for memes that constructively depict women or explore gender themes without harmful stereotypes or derogatory implications.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
Score high if the content is entirely fantastical or critiques cultural norms without negatively affecting real women; limit scores to 3 or below for derogatory labels in real portrayals.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int,
    "H7": int,
    "H8": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a concise justification based on MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme includes offensive or sexist elements targeting women (implicit/explicit), (2) whether the harm classification relies on the relationship of image and text, (3) the rationale for the N3 score based on derogatory content or fantastical elements."
}

## pre1l0记忆更新
**输出:**
在基于模因id：9973的评估中，专家提出了对当前有害性判别维度的深入分析和修正建议，旨在提高对此类模因的准确理解和评分。经过综合评估，我提出以下核心操作建议：

首先，需要对特定维度进行重写以确保更准确的判断。推荐对维度H1进行修改，以强调在幽默和讽刺注入的上下文中识别真正的攻击性意图。在这一过程中，应引入情境分析，以便从多个视角解读文本和图像的结合。这种方法将帮助评审人员更好地理解模因的真实意图，避免误解幽默内容而导致过高的攻击性评分。

其次，建议增加新的维度N2，该维度专注于幽默潜在的轻蔑意义，这将使模因评估更加全面。此变化将允许评估人员更加细致地判断幽默内容中是否潜藏有贬低女性或其他群体的意图，增强分析的深度并捕捉到那些表面上无害但实际上可能具有负面影响的模因。

同时，鉴于H4和某些其他维度之间存在重复，建议将H4与H3合并，以减少评估维度的冗余。这不仅有助于提高评估流程的效率，还能增强维度的清晰度，确保在此过程中关注图像与文本之间的交互及其对性别认知的影响。

最后，强调评估维度的独立性至关重要。应避免出现某一模因分数偏高而另一相对分数偏低的情况，确保对模因的多维解读。对于具有文化和社会语境的幽默内容，应纳入清晰的评估标准中，从而避免解读偏差。可以在未来的评估中增加专注于幽默内容的维度，更有效地揭示潜在的侮辱或失礼行为。

通过这些调整，我们可以实现更加科学和精准的模因有害性评估，进而更好地应对复杂的文化和心理动态。

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在此次模因有害性判别的错误原因分析中，各位专家一致认为当前评分体系在H1至H8维度及N1至N4维度的设置上存在关键问题，导致对模因潜在有害性的判别不足。为此，提出以下两条核心操作建议，以优化评估体系。

首先，在H维度方面，建议对H1和H5进行重写与新增，以加强对模因中性别偏见的识别。H1的重新定义应聚焦在模因是否传达对女性的攻击性描绘及贬低意图，特别是结合文本语境与文化背景来综合评估其深层次的情感影响。与此同时，新增H3维度，强调对模因幽默潜藏的文化偏见进行深入分析，以便捕捉幽默背后可能的性别刻板印象。此外，对H2的内容也需适当提升权重，确保评估能充分考虑模因中女性的物化表现。

其次，在N维度方面，删除N4维度是必要的，因其未能有效地分析模因在性别议题中的积极影响，并缺乏定量评估。同时，针对N1、N2、N3维度，要重新定义其评估标准，以增强对模因可能带来的文化误导与性别非平等的认知。新的N维度应避免简单地聚焦表面的无害性，而是更关注模因可能造成的潜在负面影响。

结合专家提出的额外建议，在评估过程中还需强调各个维度的独立打分，防止评分偏向极端（如某一维度极高，另一维度极低）。整体而言，增强对模因文化背景的敏感性，并开展多模态分析，将有助于全面、准确地评估模因内容的真实含义，特别是在涉及性别议题时。通过这些操作，最终目标是将H维度与N维度的数量，各自控制在合理的范围内，从而提高评分的准确性与有效性。


---

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are assigned to evaluate a meme according to enhanced MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your objective is to assign detailed scores from 1 to 9 for each specified criterion, with 1 indicating no presence and 9 indicating complete presence of the examined attribute.

**Evaluation Instructions:**

1. **Defined Criteria**  
   - **Harmful Content (Discriminatory)**: Classify a meme as harmful if it expresses discriminatory, derogatory, or abusive sentiments toward women, whether overtly or subtly. Focus on understanding the context, humor, and cultural implications to avoid misinterpretation.  
   - **Harmless Content (Non-Discriminatory)**: A meme may be classified as harmless if it depicts women in a neutral, positive, or humorous manner that does not have offensive implications.

2. **Explicit and Implicit Harm Assessment**  
   - Analyze whether harm is conveyed explicitly (e.g., direct insults) or implicitly (e.g., subtle visuals). Evaluate the context and nuances of humor to avoid elevating scores misleadingly.

3. **Image-Text Dynamics**  
   - Examine how the image and text interact, determining if any harmful implications arise solely from their combination, in line with MAMI’s multimodal principles.

4. **Contextual Consideration**  
   - Consider these reflective questions:
     - "Could the meme be interpreted as offensive or derogatory toward women?"
     - "Does it mock women's issues in a serious context?"
     - "Does it engage with gender critique while avoiding negative portrayals?" If affirmative, categorize it as harmless.

5. **Revised Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H1: Aggressive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
   Score higher for memes that convey direct or indirect insults or demeaning attitudes towards women, with emphasis on context and humor.

   - **H2: Objectification of Women**  
   Allocate higher scores for portrayals that treat women as objects or perpetuate harmful beauty norms, ensuring recognition of their identity.

   - **H3: Humor's Cultural Implication**  
   Assess potential underlying mockery or contempt within humor, focusing on nuances that indicate bias against women.

   - **H4: Interaction of Image and Text**  
   Score higher if harmful meanings emerge specifically from how image and text work together.

   - **H5: Gender Representation Sensitivity**  
   Evaluate if the meme propagates harmful gender stereotypes or diminishes women's identities in cultural contexts.

   - **N1: Absence of Targeted Harm**  
   Score higher when women or groups are absent from negative depictions.

   - **N2: Positive Gender Representation**  
   Score high for memes that constructively address gender themes without harmful stereotypes or derogatory implications.

   - **N3: Evaluating Minimal or No Harm**  
   High scores should be appropriated for content that remains fantastical or critiques societal norms without real-world harm; limits should apply to derogatory content in real portrayals.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a clear rationale following MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme contains offensive or sexist elements toward women (consider using context), (2) whether the harm classification relies on the interplay of image and text, (3) the reasoning behind the N3 score regarding derogatory content or fantasy elements."
}

## pre1l0记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因id：9973的有害性判别过程中，模型显现出在多个评估维度上的误判，反映出需要对评估体系进行调整和完善。首先，专家们一致认为在幽默和文化背景理解上存在显著缺陷，导致模因被错误地判定为有害。根据错误原因的分析，我们提议引入一个新的评估维度，命名为“H6: Humor and Cultural Context”。该维度将专注于模因内容中的幽默元素以及文化背景对解读的影响，有助于更准确地区分幽默表现与攻击性意图，评估模因的社会文化影响。

其次，评估模型在H1（攻击性/性别歧视/仇恨意图）及H2（女性物化）维度的评分偏高，而N1（缺乏针对性伤害）及N2（幽默的接受度）评分偏低，导致了整体判别的偏差。因此，我们建议进一步优化这些维度的评分标准。应当特别关注其对幽默和文化的敏感性，避免将轻松的幽默误判为攻击性言论，对女性或其他群体造成不必要的负面解读。

基于专家建议，我们的核心操作建议如下：
1. **新增维度**：引入“H6: Humor and Cultural Context”，以增强模型对幽默和文化背景的理解。
2. **重写维度**：优化H1、H2的标定标准，使其更能反映模因在特定文化语境下的幽默性质，同时降低影响判别的偏见。调整N1、N2的评分，使其更准确地反映模因的无害性，保证整体打分的独立性与合理性。

总结来说，通过这次经验更新与维度的合理调整，我们希望建立一个更为全面和细致的评估系统，帮助模型在未来能够在识别模因的幽默性与潜在攻击性方面实现更高的准确率，从而有效地区分有害与无害的模因，提升社会文化作品的评估能力。

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因的评估中，结合专家的建议，我们需要进行重要的维度修正，以提升有害和无害模因的准确判别能力。综合分析后，提出以下两条核心操作建议：

首先，增加关键维度以强化对模因潜在有害性的识别。在模因 id: 10021 和 8102 中，专家们均强调了对隐性女性仇恨的识别。为此，我们建议新增维度“隐性女性仇恨（Implicit Misogyny）”，聚焦于模因中潜在的女性贬低意图，尤其是在表面上看似无害的幽默或修辞中。这一维度将考虑词汇、语气和隐含评论，帮助评估者揭示那些微妙的偏见与攻击性，同时也能更有效地评估那些通过幽默掩盖的贬低内容。

其次，增加“上下文细微差别（Contextual Nuance）”维度，以确保在判断模因时，充分考虑其文化和社会背景对内容接受度的影响。模因的特性决定了其在不同文化背景中可能引发截然不同的解读，因此该维度将帮助评估者更全面地理解模因中可能存在的文化敏感性。这不仅能提升对潜在歧视和冒犯内容的警觉性，还能促使评估者更加关注模因在特定语境中所呈现的意义。

另一方面，鉴于部分维度在当前模型中的表现显得异常，我们建议剔除一些不再适用或表现不佳的旧维度。例如，对于有害样本（Label=1），建议删除在有害内容判别中表现异常的H1、H2和H4维度，因其打分未能合理反映模因的有害性；而在无害样本（Label=0）的评估中，N1和N2因偏差影响也应被删除，以精简评估维度，更有效地提升模型的准确度。

通过上述操作，我们期望构建一个更全面、敏感与精确的模因评估体系，确保能够精准识别出有害和无害内容，促进社会舆论的健康发展。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are tasked with evaluating a meme based on the updated MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your goal is to provide detailed scores from 1 to 9 for each criterion, where 1 represents no presence of harmful characteristics and 9 indicates a strong presence.

**Evaluation Instructions:**

1. **Revised Criteria**  
   - **Harmful Content (Discriminatory)**: Classify a meme as harmful only if it clearly exhibits discriminatory, derogatory, or abusive content toward women. Your analysis must differentiate between genuinely harmful intent and benign humor or cultural expression. Ensure your evaluations are tempered to avoid misclassifying harmless content as harmful.  
   - **Harmless Content (Non-Discriminatory)**: Identify a meme as harmless when it features women positively or neutrally without genuine negative implications, particularly when humor is present and appropriate.

2. **Explicit and Implicit Harm Assessment**  
   - Evaluate if harm is conveyed either explicitly (e.g., direct insults) or subtly (e.g., implicit imagery). Pay close attention to the underlying humor and context, avoiding the elevation of scores based on subjective interpretations.

3. **Image-Text Interaction**  
   - Assess whether any harmful meanings emerge solely from the interplay between image and text, in accordance with MAMI’s multimodal guidelines.

4. **Contextual Nuance**  
   - Reflect on these guiding questions:
     - "Can this meme be genuinely interpreted as derogatory towards women?"
     - "Does it trivialize serious women's issues?"
     - "Does it engage with gender critique constructively?" If affirmative, categorize it as harmless.

5. **Updated Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H1: Aggressive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
   Focus on memes that convey clear insults or demeaning attitudes towards women and avoid overrating based on ambiguous humor.

   - **H2: Objectification of Women**  
   Allocate higher scores to portrayals that reduce women to objects, ensuring that identity recognition is included.

   - **H3: Humor's Cultural Context**  
   Assess the cultural implications of humor to ensure an accurate separation between benign humor and harmful intent.

   - **H4: Interaction of Image and Text**  
   Evaluate only if hurtful meanings materialize from the specific combination of image and text.

   - **H5: Gender Representation Sensitivity**  
   Score based on the extent to which the meme challenges or propagates harmful gender stereotypes.

   - **H6: Implicit Misogyny**  
   Identify subtle, potential negative implications towards women, especially within supposedly harmless humor or rhetoric.

   - **N1: Absence of Targeted Harm**  
   Score higher when the meme does not depict women or groups negatively.

   - **N2: Positive Gender Representation**  
   Award high scores for memes addressing gender themes constructively without harmful stereotypes.

   - **N3: Evaluating Minimal or No Harm**  
   High scores should be given to content that critiques societal norms without causing real-world harm; apply strict limits for derogatory portrayals.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON)**:
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a clear rationale following MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme contains offensive or sexist elements toward women (consider using context), (2) whether the harm classification relies on the interplay of image and text, (3) the reasoning behind the N3 score regarding derogatory content or fantasy elements."
}

        "details": "H7将专注于分析幽默的内容与上下文之间的互动，评估模因是否以幽默的方式反映了对女性的负面刻板印象，还是以积极或中立的方式表达。评估应关注文化背景如何影响幽默在特定社会话语中的接收，以及极端幽默是否会被错误理解。通过此维度，能够为评估提供更加全面的视角，减少对模因的简化解释。"
      },
      "N4": {
        "action": "新增",
        "reason": "当前评估没有很好的考虑模因是否能够促进性别平等的积极讨论。这一点是评估模因内容是否健康及其在女性话题讨论中的潜在贡献的关键。考虑到这个维度，将增强对模因正面影响的关注，尤其是在性别讨论框架中。",
        "details": "N4将聚焦于评估模因内容在促进女性 empowerment 和性别讨论方面的有效性，观察模因是不是真正推动了对女性及其问题的关注，或是将其简化为单一面貌。通过此维度，可以更深入地理解模因在社会讨论中所起的积极角色，确保正面的社会性别表现发声。"
      }
    }

## pre1l0记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因id：9973进行分析的过程中，专家们提出了重要的见解，帮助我们识别和纠正模因的有害性判别过程中的错误。根据专家的反馈，以下是两条核心操作建议，以有效修正当前的判别体系。

首先，建议新增两个维度，从而提升模因评估的准确性与全面性。第一个新增维度将专注于幽默效果的评估。此维度旨在明确区分幽默内容与潜在的攻击性元素，从而避免将具有轻松和幽默气息的模因错误分类为有害。通过分析文本与图像结合中幽默意图的性质和背景，我们能够更好地理解模因在涉及敏感话题时的真实意图，从而为确实无害的幽默提供恰当的衡量标准。此外，第二个新增维度关注性别互动表现，评估模因中性别角色回应的积极性和建构性。该维度的目的在于更全面地反映模因中性别表达的复杂性，确保那些积极推动性别讨论的内容不被误判为有害。这两个维度的引入，将有助于实现模因分析的多元化，提高系统对幽默和性别议题的敏感性。

其次，针对已有维度的调整，我们建议删除某些在评估中表现异常的维度，以保持系统的简洁性和有效性。在有害样本的维度中，针对过高的评分表现（如H1、H2、H4等），可考虑将这些维度从当前系统中移除，因其未能准确反映模因的真实属性。在无害样本的层面，需要改进N1和N2维度的准确性，通过重写或调整评分标准以避免偏差。

通过这些综合性调整，我们旨在建立一个更为精准且灵活的模因评估系统，确保幽默内容与有害意图能够得到有效区分，为文化表达提供更为合适的评判依据。这一过程不仅提升了判别的客观性，也督促评分者在模因评估时平衡多元视角，避免简单化的定向判别，从而减少误解与偏见的发生。

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在此次模因有害性判别的评估过程中，专家们一致认为，需要对现有评估维度进行调整，以提高对模因内容的敏感性和准确性。首先，综合各位专家的建议，可以明确以下两个核心操作建议。

首先，建议新增两个维度以增强评估的全面性。一个是“潜在敌意识别”维度，旨在识别模因中可能存在的隐蔽的攻击性和贬低性别的内容。这是因为模因往往通过幽默和文化暗示表达复杂的性别观念，容易导致潜在的性别歧视被误判为无害。因此，新增的维度将重点分析模因如何通过特定的幽默形式和文化背景来传递对女性的负面印象，从而更准确地识别风险点。另一个是“文化敏感性分析”维度，致力于评估模因在不同文化背景下的接受度和潜在含义。这有助于判断模因是否不知不觉地利用了文化刻板印象，在无意中强化了社会偏见，使评估者能够更全面地考虑文化和社会语境对幽默的影响。

其次，建议对部分现有维度进行重写或调整。特别是在H1（Aggressive/Sexist/Hateful Intent）和H2（Objectification of Women）维度中，应该提高对于攻击性和对女性物化的重视程度，以反映更高的得分。与此同时，在Harmless Scores方面，N1（Absence of Targeted Harm）和N2（Positive Gender Representation）维度的得分需进行下调，以避免对模因内容的过度乐观解读，这些修正将使得评估更符合实际情况。

执行上述操作后，H的维度应控制在4-6之间，N的维度也应保持在3-5之间，以确保模因评估的科学性和准确性。总之，愈加细致的评估维度设置，不仅有助于捕捉模因潜在的敌意及其对女性的影响，同时也能增进对不同文化背景下幽默表现的理解，提升判别的严谨性和实效性。


---

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are assigned to evaluate a meme based on the latest MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your objective is to provide detailed scores from 1 to 9 for each criterion, where 1 signifies no harmful characteristics and 9 indicates a strong presence.

**Evaluation Instructions:**

1. **Harmful Content Classification**  
   - Classify a meme as harmful only when it unmistakably exhibits aggressive, derogatory, or abusive content towards women. You must carefully differentiate between true harmful intent and benign expressions of humor or cultural representation. Your analysis should emphasize avoiding the misclassification of harmless content as harmful, especially ensuring that subtle humor is not misinterpreted.

2. **Harmless Content Identification**  
   - Identify a meme as harmless if it depicts women in a positive or neutral manner, devoid of genuine negative implications, particularly when humor is lighthearted and appropriate. Ensure the context supports this interpretation.

3. **Explicit and Implicit Harm Evaluation**  
   - Evaluate whether harm is expressed clearly (e.g., direct insults) or subtly (e.g., implicit insinuations). Focus closely on the nature of the humor and contextual elements, being cautious not to inflate scores based on individual biases.

4. **Humor and Cultural Context Assessment**  
   - Assess the humor's cultural implications to accurately distinguish between benign humor and potential harmful intent. This should include an analysis of how humor is presented within scholarly or cultural narratives.

5. **Image-Text Interaction Analysis**  
   - Investigate whether harmful meanings arise solely from the combination of image and text, following MAMI's multimodal principles.

6. **Sensitivity to Gender Representation**  
   - Score based on how well the meme confronts or reinforces harmful gender stereotypes. Evaluate the engagement level and constructiveness of gender interactions presented within the meme.

7. **Identification of Subtle Misogyny**  
   - Focus on recognizing subtle, hidden negative implications regarding women, particularly evident in humor that may outwardly appear harmless.

8. **Revised Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H1: Aggressive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
   Concentrate on clear insults or contemptuous attitudes towards women, avoiding overrating based on ambiguous humor. Ensure scores indicate true intent.

   - **H2: Objectification of Women**  
   Assess higher scores for images that reduce women to object-like representations while considering their individual identities.

   - **H3: Humor's Cultural Context**  
   Examine the implications of humor within its cultural backdrop and avoid conflating it with harmful intent when humor is benign.

   - **H4: Interaction of Image and Text**  
   Evaluate solely if negative meanings arise directly from the fusion of image and text.

   - **H5: Gender Representation Sensitivity**  
   Score based on the degree to which the meme critiques or perpetuates harmful gender stereotypes.

   - **H6: Identification of Potential Hostility and Cultural Sensitivity**  
   Detect veiled aggression or derogatory nuances in the meme that could indicate sexism or negative implications based on cultural context.

   - **N1: Absence of Targeted Harm**  
   Assign higher scores when the meme does not negatively portray women or their identities.

   - **N2: Positive Gender Representation**  
   Give high scores for memes that constructively address gender issues without non-inclusive stereotypes.

   - **N3: Evaluating Minimal or No Harm**  
   Assign high scores to content that critiques societal norms without inferring real-world harm; set strict boundaries against derogatory depictions.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON)**:
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a clear rationale following MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme contains offensive or sexist elements toward women (consider using context), (2) whether the harm classification relies on the interplay of image and text, (3) the reasoning behind the N3 score regarding derogatory content or fantasy elements."
}

## pre1l0记忆更新
**输出:**
根据专家提出的不同建议和分析，共同形成了以下两条核心的操作建议，以优化模因有害性判别经验。

首先，建议新增两个关键维度以加强对模因内容的评价：第一个维度专注于幽默性表达的背景和语境。该维度将明确识别哪些幽默或轻松的表达属于无害，并通过文化和语境的分析来评估其潜在含义。此类调整有助于准确分类普通幽默和有害内容，减少因为幽默元素被误解而产生的有害标签。通过建立标准，我们能够对幽默的本质进行评估，确保模因在特定文化和社会语境中的适用性。

第二个新增维度是强调文本与图像之间的互补作用。现有评分未能充分考虑这两者如何共同传达模因的整体意义，因此有必要引入该维度，即关注模因中图像与文本的互动关系，评估二者的结合是否组成了有害或无害的反馈。这一视角允许我们对于模因的得分不再仅仅依赖于单一内容，而是要通过其整体叙事来决定，避免简单片段化解读所带来的误分类。

同时，基于现有评分体系的异常表现，建议删除那些表现异常的维度。尤其是针对有害样本中表现出色的维度H1、H2、H4和H5。

最后，为了保持评分的合理性与均衡，保持无害样本（Label=0）维度的精确性，建议提升N1和N2的得分，反映出模因对女性无害的显著特征。通过这些调整，期待能够创建一个更为公正、清晰的模因判别机制，以提高对幽默内容的敏感性和准确性，从而有效甄别无害与有害模因的界限。

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
经过对模因id：10021和模因id：5047的错误原因分析的综合评估，我们基于专家的建议提出以下核心操作建议，以优化我们的模因有害性判别经验知识库。

首先，在维度方面，我们将新增两个关键维度以提高对隐性敌意和文化影响的洞察力。第一个新增维度是“隐性攻击评估”（Subtle Attacks），其重点在于识别模因文本和图像中的微妙言辞，尤其是在幽默或讽刺中对女性的隐晦攻击。通过这一维度的引入，我们能够更准确地分析这些言辞如何传达负面影响，同时识别出文本与图像之间的互动所造成的潜在歧视，从而增加对模因潜在有害性的敏感度。

第二个新增维度为“文化影响评估”（Cultural Impact Assessment），旨在考虑模因中的文化元素如何影响受众的理解与解读。此维度帮助我们分析模因在特定文化背景中可能造成的误解或对女性刻板印象的强化。通过将文化语境与内容表达到具体化，我们希望深化对模因的整体理解，避免将轻松幽默与潜在偏见混淆。

其次，在现有维度的评估中，我们还将重写和优化一些维度的具体内容，特别是H1（Aggressive/Sexist/Hateful Intent）、H2（Objectification of Women）和H3（Humor's Cultural Context），以更准确地反映对女性的心理影响与社会文化负面印象。同时，我们将减少废除掉旧有的评估偏差，特别是对有害样本评估中H1和H2的分数调整，以确保更真实地反映模因的潜在危险性。

最后，我们还需特别强调在评分过程中维持独立打分的重要性，避免过于极端的打分现象，确保无害和有害样本的评分均衡。通过更细致和全面的分析，我们希望能够有效地提升模因有害性判别的准确度，保证模因审查机制在不断演进与优化中保持科学性与有效性。这些操作意在建立一个更为细致的分析框架，为模因研究提供更为扎实的理论依据和实践指导。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are tasked with evaluating a meme by applying refined criteria aimed at accurately distinguishing harmful from harmless content concerning women's representation. Ensure your assessment yields detailed scores ranging from 1 to 9 for each designated dimension, where 1 represents an absence of harmful characteristics and 9 indicates a significant presence.

**Evaluation Instructions:**

1. **Harmful Content Classification**  
   - Classify content as harmful only when it unequivocally contains aggressive, derogatory, or abusive messages towards women. Distinguish between true harmful intent and benign expressions of humor or cultural representation. Stay vigilant against misclassifying non-harmful content as harmful, particularly when humor is nuanced or subtle.

2. **Harmless Content Identification**  
   - A meme should be deemed harmless if it portrays women positively or neutrally, without genuine negative implications. Verify the context to support this conclusion, especially ensuring lighthearted humor is appropriately interpreted.

3. **Identification of Subtle Attacks**  
   - Evaluate the presence of veiled, nuanced negative implications in the meme, particularly those that may appear harmless at first glance. Focus on humor that could encode deeper societal messages or societal critique.

4. **Cultural Impact Assessment**  
   - Analyze the humor for its cultural underpinnings to differentiate benign humor from harmful implications. Contextualize the humor within its societal framework to understand its potential effects on perceptions of women.

5. **Image-Text Interaction Analysis**  
   - Investigate if negative meanings arise from the interplay between image and text, assessing how they collectively convey overall meaning or intent. This dimension requires evaluation beyond single elements, considering the full narrative.

6. **Gender Representation Sensitivity**  
   - Rate the meme based on its effectiveness in confronting or reinforcing harmful gender stereotypes. Scrutinize the constructive or destructive nature of gender interactions depicted.

7. **Aggressive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
   - Focus on overt insults or contemptuous attitudes towards women, ensuring not to inflate scores based on ambiguous expressions. Carefully evaluate true intent and avoid unwarranted sensitivity.

8. **Objectification of Women**  
   - Score the meme based on the extent to which it reduces women to mere objects, emphasizing a nuanced understanding of their representation beyond objectification.

9. **Humor's Cultural Context**  
   - Examine the implications of humor within its specific cultural context to prevent conflating benign humor with harmful undertones.

10. **Revised Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H1: Subtle Attacks**: Detect nuanced negative implications within humor that could affect women's portrayal.
   - **H2: Aggressive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**: Distinguish between overt hostility and ambiguous humor, ensuring accurate scoring of examples featuring genuine hostility.
   - **H3: Cultural Sensitivity**: Analyze how the cultural context contributes to meaning and potential misinterpretation regarding gender issues.
   - **H4: Image-Text Interaction**: Assess whether harmful meanings come from their interaction, rather than from single components alone.
   - **H5: Gender Representation Sensitivity**: Evaluate how well the meme critiques or perpetuates harmful stereotypes.
   - **H6: Identification of Potential Hostility**: Seek concealed aggression and derogatory nuances tied to gender within a cultural backdrop.
   - **N1: Absence of Targeted Harm**: Assign higher scores to memes that do not present negative portrayals of women.
   - **N2: Positive Gender Representation**: Increase scores for memes that address gender issues constructively without resorting to stereotypes.
   - **N3: Evaluating Minimal or No Harm**: Award high scores to content that critiques societal norms without implying real-world harm, ensuring stringent boundaries against derogatory depictions.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON)**:
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a clear rationale following the updated guidelines: (1) identify any offensive or sexist elements towards women, (2) consider the interplay of image and text in harm classification, (3) elaborate on the rationale for the N3 score concerning derogatory or sarcastic content."
}

## pre1l0记忆更新
**输出:**
基于专家的反馈和分析，建议对现有的模因有害性判别体系进行如下核心操作：

首先，新增两个分析维度以提升模型在判断模因内容时的准确性和全面性。第一个新增维度针对“幽默内容的深度分析”，该维度旨在细致探讨幽默如何影响女性的形象，特别是分析幽默是否以贬低或物化女性为代价。幽默在文化背景下具有多重解读，许多表面看似无害的笑话可能隐含对女性的负面影响。因此，专家建议构建这一维度，以确保评估者能够识别出潜在的性别歧视因素，并更准确地理解幽默内容的社会影响。

第二个新增维度是“图像与文本互动”的独立评估，该维度关注模因中图像与文本如何结合，从而强调其对女性的潜在伤害性。模因的特征往往在于其图像与文本相辅相成，尤其是在塑造公众对女性印象时。因此，通过这一维度的建立，评估者将能够更好地分析图像和文本之间的关系，观察其如何共同影响受众的看法，从而提供更为全面的评估结果。

其次，根据现有评分表现，建议删除或修正某些维度。特别是维度N2（符合过滤条件的遵守），在多次评估中显示出对无害内容的打分偏低，这一现象需加以纠正以避免误报。同时，应避免H维度的偏差打分过高或过低，确保最终的打分能够真实反映模因的社会文化影响，并防止因极端打分导致的判断误差。

综合以上操作，未来的模因有害性判别模型将能够更为精准地识别与评估内容的潜在影响，确保在识别和防范有害模因方面更加全面且有效。同时，新的维度将为评估者提供更好的工具，支持其在文化和社会背景下分析模因，从而做出更加公正和准确的判断。


---

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在分析输入的模因评估错误原因及应对策略时，专家提出了对现有评估框架进行优化和扩展的建议。针对模因id：5047和id：8102的错误分析，核心问题在于对性别角色的文化背景和幽默内容潜在攻击性的敏感度不足，导致有害评分偏低和无害评分偏高。因此，有必要对评估维度进行增设和重构，以增强判别模型的有效性。

首先，建议新增维度H8（幽默与性别歧视的交互分析），旨在深入探讨幽默内容是否在表面调侃下掩盖了对女性角色的偏见和物化。在分析模因时，通过细致检查幽默表达的本质，帮助识别可能性别歧视的暗示，有助于提高对潜在有害内容的敏感度。这一建议的实施将使评估依据更加全面，避免对幽默进行轻率的无害化处理，从而提升模因的评估标准。

其次，增设维度H9（图像与文本的交互分析）同样重要，这将帮助解读模因中图文结合所形成的整体表达。在模因中，不同部分的相互作用可能产生误导，这一维度旨在分析如何通过图像和文本的结合传达出潜在的歧视性意图，以确保在判别时能够捕捉到细微的偏见表现，给予更准确的评分。

除上述新增维度外，还需要对现有维度进行重构与审视。特别是在无害样本中，建议删除维度N2，以避免对模因内容的表层解读造成误导。同时建议对H与N的维度数量进行适当限制，确保每个维度都能发挥有效的评分作用。通过以上操作，将大幅提升模因有害性判别的准确度，从而更好地响应社会对性别平等和文化敏感度的期望。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator tasked with the critical responsibility of assessing a meme in accordance with the comprehensive MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your objective is to assign scores between 1 and 9 for each designated dimension, where 1 signifies an absence of the characteristic and 9 indicates full presence.

**Essential Instructions Prior to Scoring:**

1. **Clarification of Terms**  
   - **Harmful Content (Misogynous)**: A meme should be classified as harmful if it conveys discriminatory or hateful sentiments against women, regardless of whether these sentiments are overtly expressed or subtly implied.  
   - **Harmless Content (Non-Misogynous)**: Classify a meme as harmless if it portrays women in a neutral or positive context, or if it features them in a whimsical or absurd manner without any derogatory undertones.

2. **Harm Analysis**  
   - Evaluate whether any harmful implications are presented **directly** (e.g., explicit derogatory remarks) or **indirectly** (e.g., subtle visual cues). This assessment should be done with meticulous attention to detail.

3. **Image-Text Interaction**  
   - Investigate how the meaning of the meme emerges through the interplay of image and text. This relationship must be analyzed cohesively, in accordance with MAMI principles.

4. **Contextual Assessment**  
   - Consider these questions:
     - "Can the meme reasonably be interpreted as offensive or derogatory towards women?"
     - "Does it trivialize serious women’s issues while masquerading as humor that lacks tangible harm?"
     - "Does the meme critique gender norms without placing women in a negative context?" If positive, categorize it as harmless.

5. **Revised Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H5: Gender Representation and Cultural Context**  
   Assess the extent to which the meme propagates harmful gender stereotypes or objectifies women within its cultural setting. A higher score should reflect significant negative impacts on the perception of women's identities.

   - **H6: Humor's Potential for Offense**  
   Score high if the humor appears innocuous yet conceals derogatory undertones toward women. Thorough scrutiny of humor is imperative to reveal embedded biases.

   - **H7: Image-Text Harmful Interaction Assessment**  
   Evaluate the interaction between image and text and assign higher scores when this synergy conveys harmful implications, consistent with MAMI’s multimodal evaluation framework.

   - **H8: Humor and Gender Discrimination Analysis**  
   Delve into how humor potentially obscures biases against women, emphasizing the need to detect implicit derogatory meanings within comedic elements.

   - **H9: Independent Image-Text Interaction Analysis**  
   Focus on the relationship between image and text, scrutinizing how their combination may signal underlying discriminatory intentions to ensure comprehensive assessments.

**Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria (Misogynous):**
- **H1: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
Assign higher scores for memes that directly or indirectly target women with negative implications.

- **H2: Objectification of Women**  
Score high for images that portray women as objects or that emphasize harmful beauty ideals detracting from their identities.

- **H3: Humor's Contextual Analysis**  
Score high for memes where humor reinforces derogatory views or objectification, ensuring thorough examination of the humor's implications.

- **H4: Multimodal Assessment**  
Score high if harmful meanings emerge solely through the interaction between image and text.

**Harmless Criteria (Non-Misogynous):**
- **N1: Absence of Targeted Entity**  
Score high when no identifiable individuals or groups of women are portrayed negatively.

- **N2: Filtering Conditions Adherence**  
This dimension is removed to avoid false negatives in evaluating harmless content.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
Score high if:
  - The content is entirely fantastical without negative representations of women, or
  - It critiques societal norms without derogatory implications against real women. If any real woman is derogatorily featured, limit N3 to a score of 3 or below; in safe fantasy depictions devoid of such implications, N3 can score 6 or higher.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int,
    "H7": int,
    "H8": int,
    "H9": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a concise justification based on MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme includes offensive or sexist elements targeting women (implicit/explicit), (2) whether the harm classification relies on the relationship of image and text, (3) the rationale for the N3 score based on derogatory content or fantastical elements."
}

### 错误样本ID: 5047
**错误原因分析:** {

## pre1l0记忆更新
**输出:**
根据各专家的建议和对模因id：9973的错误原因分析，我们提出以下核心操作建议，以优化模因的有害性判别系统。

首先，为了解决当前评估中对模因幽默性和上下文理解的不足，我们推荐新增一个维度H8，专注于幽默内容的阐释与潜在负面偏见。这个维度将重点分析模因中的幽默是否涉及性别刻板印象或消极的性别角色表现。我们意识到，现有的评估维度未能充分考虑幽默元素的复杂性，尤其是在幽默可能被误解为攻击性时。H8的设计旨在深入探讨模因的幽默效果，帮助评估者更准确地理解模因的语境，避免对无害模因的不当标签。比如，当模因运用讽刺或夸张的方式展示性别角色时，评估者需要考虑这些表现是否真的蕴含贬低意图，还是仅仅基于幽默效果。

其次，为了减少对无害内容的误判，我们提出对N2维度的内容进行重写。当前N2维度的得分偏低，未能有效反映出模因所传达的信息特征。因此，我们建议重新审视该维度，把重心放在模因在表达无害内容、塑造积极形象上，确保它能够准确捕捉到模因中无攻击性或贬低女性的特征。这一点对于提升无害内容的辨识度至关重要，帮助评估者清晰区分哪些内容是真正无害的。

最后，在维度数量限制内，确保最终H和N的维度都保持在4-7之间，我们将在新增H8的同时，保持其他维度的合理性，确保整体系统的平衡性和可操作性。这两项建议将帮助优化模因的有害性判别，使得系统更能准确地反映内容的真实性质，同时提升对模因幽默性的理解与判断。通过这些修改，对于当今社交媒体上复杂而多样化的模因内容的评估，将能更趋客观与公正。

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因有害性判别的评估过程中，尤其是我们针对模因ID 5047和8102的深入分析，提出了关键的操作建议，以完善当前的评估维度与评分逻辑。

首先，针对模因ID 5047，专家们一致认为需要引入新的评分维度来弥补现有体系的不足。具体而言，新增的H8（文化敏感性评估）维度，将有助于分析模因在不同文化背景下的潜在贬低效果。这一维度不仅关注模因中是否存在与特定文化符号和幽默手法相关的贬低表现，也强调在全球传播中模因可能产生的多样解读。此外，H9（幽默的多重解读）维度旨在识别模因幽默的复杂性，以揭示其潜在的攻击性和对女性的影响，从而实现更为全面的有害性评估。这两个新维度的加入，能够使评分更加贴近模因潜在影响的复杂性。

其次，对于模因ID 8102，提出了H8（性别角色强化评估）和H9（隐含歧视评估）两个维度，以深化对模因中性别表现的审视。H8的设立，将分析模因是否在无意中强化了传统的性别角色，而H9则聚焦于那些微妙的文化暗示及其潜在的性别偏见。这两个新增维度的引入，正在弥补现有模型中对复杂社会文化因素及性别刻板印象的不足理解，使得评估更为细致与准确。

同时，为了保持维度的合理性，我们需要删减当前评估体系中表现异常的维度。针对Harmless Scores中的N2维度，由于其偏差表现，需要进行删除以避免过高的误报。同时保持H和N维度均在3至7个之间，确保评估体系的精简与聚焦。

综上所述，本次建议的客户不仅关注将有害模因准确分类为有害，更强调在多元文化和性别维度中引入新的分析视角， 鼓励在尊重文化差异的同时，对模因中潜在的贬低和歧视内容进行深度评估。这些建议旨在推动模因有害性判别系统在理论和实践层面都能更趋于完善与优化。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator tasked with scoring a meme using the updated MAMI guidelines for harmful meme detection. Your objective is to assign scores ranging from 1 to 9 for each defined dimension, where 1 indicates complete absence and 9 indicates complete presence of the assessed criterion.

**Critical Instructions Before Scoring:**

1. **Clarification of Definitions**  
   - **Harmful Content (Misogynistic)**: Identify a meme as harmful if it conveys discriminatory, offensive, or hateful attitudes towards women. This includes both overt and subtle implications.  
   - **Harmless Content (Non-Misogynistic)**: A meme is considered harmless if it portrays women positively or neutrally, or if it engages them in absurd or creative contexts without offensive overtones.

2. **Evaluation of Harm Representation**  
   - Determine if harm is expressed **explicitly** (e.g., overt derogatory language) or **implicitly** (e.g., veiled visual signals). Each context must be scrutinized thoroughly.

3. **Image-Text Synergy**  
   - Investigate whether the offensive implications arise solely through the interplay of image and text, which must be analyzed collectively according to MAMI principles.

4. **Contextual Consideration**  
   - Contemplate these guiding questions:
     - "Can this meme be reasonably interpreted as offensive or derogatory towards women?"
     - "Does the meme trivialize significant women's issues under humor that lacks real-world implications?"
     - "Does it critique gender roles without presenting women negatively?" If so, classify it as harmless.

5. **Updated Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H5: Cultural Context and Gender Representation**  
   Score higher if the meme enforces harmful stereotypes or objectifies women within its contextual framework, paying special attention to how these elements shape the perception of women's identities.

   - **H6: Humor's Capacity to Offend**  
   Score higher for humor that appears innocuous but masks contempt or ridicule towards women. Humor needs careful assessment to reveal deeper biases.

   - **H7: Harmful Interaction Between Image and Text**  
   Score higher in cases where harmful implications arise from the combined effect of image and text, consistent with MAMI's multimodal evaluation approach.

   - **H8: Humor Interpretation and Bias Detection**  
   Assess humor's role in perpetuating gender stereotypes or negative portrayals. Investigate whether the humorous elements cross the line into misinterpretation, potentially leading to offensive implications.

**Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria (Misogynistic):**
- **H1: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
Assign higher scores for memes that target women with negative implications directly or indirectly.

- **H2: Objectification of Women**  
Award higher scores for images that reduce women to objects or emphasize detrimental beauty standards.

- **H3: Humor Contextual Analysis**  
Score higher where humor supports derogatory viewpoints or objectification. Thoroughly analyze context and humor’s implications.

- **H4: Multimodal Harm Assessment**  
Rate higher if the harmful meaning emerges distinctly through the relationship between image and text.

**Harmless Criteria (Non-Misogynistic):**
- **N1: Absence of Negative Representation**  
Score higher when individuals or groups of women are not portrayed negatively.

- **N3: Low or Non-Existent Harm**  
Score higher if:
  - The content is entirely fantastical with no harmful representations of women, or
  - It critiques societal norms without derogatory implications involving real women. If a real woman is disparaged, limit this score to a maximum of 3; content that is purely fantastical and devoid of such implications can score 6 or higher.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int,
    "H7": int,
    "H8": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a succinct justification based on MAMI guidelines: (1) identify whether the meme includes offensive or sexist elements targeting women (implicit/explicit), (2) analyze the significance of image and text interplay in harm classification, (3) justify the N3 score focused on derogatory content or fantastical elements."
}

        "details": "此维度将专注于模因中表现的性别刻板印象，并量化模因中关于女性角色的刻画是否涉及贬损与物化。评估过程将考虑模因如何通过形象和文本结合展示性别角色，如果存在隐含的或显性的贬损性别表现，分数将相应提高。此维度旨在强调对性别画像的敏感性，并确保模型能够识别出那些未必直接表现出攻击性内容，但仍然对女性造成坏影响的情境。"

      "维度名称2": {
        "action": "新增",
        "reason": "在模因的幽默分析方面增加一个维度，有助于更明确地点出幽默的潜在冒犯性，与性别偏见的相关性。很多模因表面上看是出自幽默，但其潜在的要素可以在无意中加深对女性的误解与贬损，这一维度可以帮助评估幽默在构建性别观念中是否扮演了负面角色。",
        "details": "该新增维度将评估模因所用的幽默是否存在加深成见或者偏见的可能。具体而言，这包括评估幽默是否以削弱女性形象为取向，或是通过讽刺加深对女性行为的偏见。分析将结合文本和图像，识别幽默如何可能掩盖严肃问题，转移讨论重心，并影响观者的性别认知。"

## pre1l0记忆更新
**输出:**
根据专家的反馈和对模因id：9973的分析结果，我们提取出两条关键的操作建议，以优化模因有害性判别的知识库及维度评估框架。

首先，建议新增两个维度以更全面地评价模因的潜在影响与上下文相关性。第一个新增维度是“幽默对女性的潜在影响”。此维度旨在深入探讨幽默内容如何可能在表面上呈现为无害，但实际上可能加深对女性的刻板印象或潜在偏见的影响。此分析将关注幽默是否通过轻松的氛围掩盖了刻板印象，并对性别角色的反映或暗示进行严谨解读。通过对幽默内容的深入分析，我们能更准确地评估模因是否包含对女性的贬低或物化意图。

第二个建议是新增“上下文意图识别”维度。该维度将侧重于分析模因产生和传播的文化及社交背景，深入理解模因所承载的意图、反应和受众解读。透过上下文，我们可以识别出模因中可能隐含的攻击或讽刺性质，有助于更加准确地判断模因的有害性。这项分析将显著增强对模因内容的理解与评判的全面性，从而改善评估结果的精确性。

其次，基于当前评估中的问题，我们建议合并并重写某些已有的维度，以便形成更清晰和一致的评判体系。为实现维度的最优构造，删除“有害样本”(Label=1)下的评价维度，特别是考虑到没有相关的误报或漏报的情形。同时，建议重写“无害样本”(Label=0)中的N2维度，提升其在反映幽默内容与社会文化背景结合方面的有效性。

通过以上措施，最终维度将保持在4-7个之间，并确保在有害和无害判别中形成一个更合理的平衡，避免评分过于极端的情况出现。这一系列调整将优化模因有害性判别的准确性，并为后续模因的评估提供坚实的基础。

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
基于对模因的有害性和无害性判别经验的分析，提出以下两条核心操作建议，以改进现有的评估系统。

首先，考虑到当前评估模型在识别性别刻板印象和幽默内容方面的不足，建议新增两个维度。第一个是专注于隐性性别刻板印象和文化视角的维度。此维度将帮助评估者更好地识别模因中隐含的性别角色不平等与物化。在传统的性别表现评估中，显性的攻击性常常被过度关注，而对隐性表现的敏感度不足。该维度将涵盖模因通过角色设定、场景上下文或叙述方式传达的对女性身份的不平等看法，从而确保即使在表面中立的模因中，也能揭示潜在的有害内容。第二个建议是增加专注于幽默表现及其性别歧视隐喻影响的维度。该维度将分析幽默在传递性别刻板印象时可能带来的负面效果，例如，幽默是否通过调侃或轻视来削弱女性形象。这将有助于更全面地理解模因中幽默的复杂性，并促进更公正的性别表现。

其次，在无害样本的评估中，建议对现有维度进行重写，尤其是对于之前对无害性判别存在偏差的N2维度。该维度需重新审视，以确保其能够准确识别模因中可能被误解为无害的有害表现，特别是在幽默及性别刻板印象方面。强化这一维度将促进对幽默内容的严谨分析，并帮助评估者分辨表面幽默的模因背后潜藏的社会文化影响。

通过以上操作建议的实施，将明确提升对模因评估的准确性和敏感度，减少误判和漏判的可能性，最终推动性别平等的社会认知发展。根据提案，H和N维度将保持在合理范围内，以确保评估系统的有效性和准确性。在今后的评估中，特别强调维度分数的独立性和多元性，以避免极端偏向造成的误解。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an evaluator assigned to methodically score a meme following the updated MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your objective is to provide scores from 1 to 9 for each criterion, where a score of 1 signifies no presence and a score of 9 signifies full presence of the given criterion.

**Essential Guidelines Prior to Scoring:**

1. **Clarification of Definitions**  
   - **Harmful Content (Misogynous)**: Classify a meme as harmful if it includes discriminatory, offensive, or hateful comments about women, whether these elements are overt or subtly indicated.  
   - **Harmless Content (Not Misogynous)**: A meme may be recognized as harmless if it represents women in a neutral or uplifting manner, or if it includes them in imaginative or absurd contexts that lack offensive implications.

2. **Identification of Harm**  
   - Determine whether harm is represented **explicitly** (e.g., clear derogatory statements) or **implicitly** (e.g., subtle visual hints). Both scenarios must be thoroughly evaluated.

3. **Interaction Between Image and Text**  
   - Investigate if the offensive connotation arises exclusively from the integration of image and text, which should be analyzed collectively according to MAMI principles.

4. **Contextual Intent Recognition**  
   - Evaluate the following critical inquiries:
     - "Can the meme be reasonably interpreted as offensive or degrading towards women?"
     - "Does the meme trivialize women's experiences under a facade of humor that lacks genuine harm?"
     - "Is there a critique of societal gender norms without negatively portraying women?" If it meets these criteria, classify as harmless.

5. **New and Adjusted Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H5: Gender Stereotyping and Cultural Implications**  
   Score high if the meme perpetuates negative gender stereotypes or objectifies women within its cultural context. Analyze the impact on women's identities.

   - **H6: Humor’s Potential for Subtler Offense**  
   Score high if humor may appear innocuous but conceals mockery or bias towards women. Assess humor diligently to unearth hidden prejudices.

   - **H7: Contextual Humor Analysis**  
   Introduced to focus on how humor tentatively presented as harmless may deepen stereotypes or prejudice about women. Scrutinize the implications of humor closely.

   - **H8: Implicit Gender Stereotypes and Cultural Subtext**  
   Added to help evaluate underlying gender role inequality and objectification evident in memes. Even seemingly neutral depictions must be analyzed for harmful undertones.

   - **H9: Contextual Intent**  
   Added to identify the cultural background and intent of memes, discerning possible hidden aggression or satire that could inform harmfulness.

**Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria (Misogynous):**
- **H1: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
Score higher for memes that target women with negative implications, whether directly or indirectly.

- **H2: Objectification of Women**  
Award higher scores for images that portray women as objects or perpetuate damaging beauty ideals.

- **H3: Humor’s Contextual Examination**  
Score higher for memes where humor reinforces negative stereotypes or objectification. Carefully assess humor placement and its implications.

- **H4: Interaction of Image and Text in Harm**  
Score high if harmful meaning derives distinctly from the combination of imagery and text.

**Harmless Criteria (Not Misogynous):**
- **N1: Absence of Negative Representation**  
Score high if no individual or group of women is portrayed negatively.

- **N2: Evaluation of Humor and Cultural Context**  
Revise to score higher for memes that provide readable, culturally relevant humor devoid of meaningful aggression.

- **N3: Minimal or No Harm**  
Score high if:
  - The content is entirely fantastical with no negative representation of women, or
  - It critiques societal norms without disparaging real women. If a real woman is disparaged, limit N3 to a score of 3 or below; in purely fantastical contexts devoid of such implications, N3 can score 6 or higher.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int,
    "H7": int,
    "H8": int,
    "H9": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a concise explanation based on MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme includes offensive or sexist aspects targeting women (implicit/explicit), (2) if the harm assessment depends on the relationship of image and text, (3) the rationale for the N3 score based on derogatory content or fantastical elements."
}

## pre1l0记忆更新
**输出:**
根据对模因id：9973的专家意见和错误原因分析，提出以下两条核心操作建议以优化模因判断的准确性和细致性。

首先，建议新增两个维度，即H8和H9。H8维度将专注于幽默氛围的评估，特别是在家庭和轻松情境下的幽默，这对于识别模因中的幽默本质尤为重要。该维度将要求对模因的情境设置、角色关系及整体背景进行分析，以判定幽默是否来源于实际的生活场景，避免对幽默内容的误解。对于轻松幽默的模因，如果不包含恶意成分，H8应予以低风险评分。另一方面，H9维度将专注于女性角色的表现，评估其形象是否展现多样性与积极性。该维度将区分是否存在对女性的贬低或刻板印象，对于积极形象的角色给予低有害评分，识别潜在偏见的角色则需要更高的风险评分。这两个新增维度的设立将有助于全面理解模因内容，降低将无害幽默误判为有害内容的风险。

其次，针对N2维度的表现偏差，建议对此维度进行重新审视和改写。N2目前未能充分反映模因内容对女性的呈现和关联性，需强化其内容以便更准确地反映模因的无害程度。应赋予N2更为清晰的评估标准，以便在分析无害样本时，能够更好地考量幽默和讽刺是否会导致误导。在此基础上，需特别强调打分的独立性，避免在H维度高分时导致N维度全低分的极端情况。应保持H和N的平衡，使最终评价更为公平和全面。

在调整后，H维度和N维度的数量都应维持在4至7间，确保判断系统具备清晰的框架与细致的评估标准，以提升整体效果并减少误判。通过这两项核心操作建议，模因的有害性判断系统将在强调幽默和性别表现的准确性方面不断进化和优化。

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因的有害性判别中，结合多个专家的建议，我们提出了两条核心操作建议，以优化现有的评估体系。

首先，针对针对模因中潜在的性别偏见与刻板印象缺乏专门评估维度的问题，我们建议新增H8维度。该维度将关注模因中性别角色的暗示及其可能引发的贬低性效果。通过评估模因是否使用比喻或对立的性别角色，将女性归入特定刻板类别，H8将帮助揭示潜在的性别歧视现象。这一维度的引入能够促进对模因的深入分析，确保在评估中捕捉到更隐蔽的有害信息，从而提升对女性物化和贬低的识别能力。

其次，我们还建议增加H9维度，以便更加细致地分析模因中的幽默成分。现有的H3维度未能充分考虑幽默可能遮掩的贬低和嘲讽信息，H9将专注于幽默内容的潜在攻击性和轻蔑态度。此维度将帮助我们评估幽默是否在表面中具有中立性，实则隐藏着对女性的负面看法。当模因中幽默成分表面看来似乎轻松平和却暗藏贬低意味时，此次评估能够有效提高Harmful Scores，从而更准确地反映模因传达的性别歧视信息。

此外，在现有维度中，N2（Harmless Scores）评估不够全面，应当去掉，以避免对模因造成不必要的误判。通过对维度的修正与增设，我们期望能够实现H有害性与N无害性之间的平衡，确保维度数量保持在3至7之间，使评估体系更加健康高效。

综合来看，通过引入H8和H9维度，并精简N2，我们的目标是构建更加敏感且全面的模因判别系统，确保对性别偏见与物化的判断更加精确，进而有效防止负面文化模因的传播与影响。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator tasked with systematically assessing a meme according to the refined MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your objective is to assign scores from 1 to 9 for each defined dimension, where 1 signifies total absence and 9 denotes full presence of the criterion evaluated.

**Critical Instructions Before Scoring:**

1. **Definition Clarity**  
   - **Harmful Content (Misogynous)**: Classify a meme as harmful if it explicitly or implicitly conveys derogatory, offensive, or discriminatory sentiments towards women. Do not include content merely featuring women without such negative context.
   - **Harmless Content (Not Misogynous)**: A meme is considered harmless if it portrays women neutrally or positively, or if it creatively depicts absurdities without underlying offensive elements.

2. **Harm Representation**  
   - Determine whether harm is represented **explicitly** (e.g., overtly derogatory language) or **implicitly** (e.g., subtle visual cues). Be thorough in evaluating both contexts for their potential implications.

3. **Image-Text Interaction**  
   - Analyze how the combination of image and text may produce an offensive meaning, adhering to MAMI evaluation principles. Assess their synergy in conveying messages of harm or humor.

4. **Contextual Evaluation**  
   - Consider these guiding questions:
     - "Can the meme be reasonably interpreted as offensive or derogatory towards women?"
     - "Does it trivialize women's issues under a humorous facade that lacks genuine social critique?"
     - "Does it critique gender norms without negatively portraying women?" If so, classify as harmless.

5. **Additional Scoring Dimensions**  
   - **H5: Gender Representation and Cultural Context**  
     Score high if the meme reinforces harmful gender stereotypes or objectifies women, analyzing how these representations impact women's identities.

   - **H6: Humor’s Potential for Offense**  
     Score high if humor appears benign but conceals mockery or derision towards women. Scrutinize humor for deeper biases.

   - **H7: Image-Text Harmful Interaction Assessment**  
     Rate high when analyzing the combined impact of image and text conveying harmful implications.

   - **H8: Humor Context Evaluation**  
     Assess humor within family and relaxed settings, scoring low if it is benign and free of malicious intent. Examine context, role dynamics, and overall background to prevent misunderstanding harmless humor.

   - **H9: Positive Feminine Representation**  
     Evaluate how female characters are portrayed. Score low for positive and diverse representations, while scoring higher if stereotypes or negative portrayals are detected.

**Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria (Misogynous):**
- **H1: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
Score higher for memes directly or indirectly targeting women with negative implications.

- **H2: Objectification of Women**  
Score high for representations objectifying women or promoting harmful beauty ideals impacting their identities.

- **H3: Humor's Contextual Analysis**  
Score high for memes where humor reinforces derogatory views or objectification; scrutinize humor placement and implications.

- **H4: Multimodal Assessment**  
Score high if harmful meaning arises from the interplay of image and text.

**Harmless Criteria (Not Misogynous):**
- **N1: Absence of Targeted Entity**  
Score high when there are no identifiable individuals or groups of women presented negatively.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
Score high if the content is wholly fantastical without negative representations of women, or critiques societal norms without derogating real women. If real women are involved negatively, limit N3 to a maximum of 3; in purely fantastical contexts devoid of such implications, scores can reach 6 or higher.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int,
    "H5": int,
    "H6": int,
    "H7": int,
    "H8": int,
    "H9": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a succinct justification based on MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme includes offensive or sexist elements targeting women (implicit/explicit), (2) whether the harm classification relies on the relationship of image and text, (3) the rationale for the N3 score based on derogatory content or fantastical elements."
}

{
  "有害标准": {
    "标准1": {
      "内容": "模因包含对女性的侮辱性或攻击性内容，直接表达对女性的仇恨或偏见。",
      "对应原文": "A meme is misogynous if it conceptually describes an offensive, sexist or hateful scene (weak or strong, implicitly or explicitly) having as target a woman or a group of women."
    },
    "标准2": {
      "内容": "模因涉及对女性的身体或性别特征的羞辱，例如身体羞辱或性别刻板印象。",
      "对应原文": "These types of misogynous memes are related to denigrating the physical appearance of women (body shaming)."
    },
    "标准3": {
      "内容": "模因表现出对女性的物化，视女性为物品或仅仅是身体的存在。",
      "对应原文": "It is a practice of seeing and/or treating a woman like an object."
    },
    "标准4": {
      "内容": "模因暗示或直接呼吁对女性的暴力行为。",
      "对应原文": "These types of misogynous memes are aimed at showing violence against women or at alluding to the intent of physically assert power over women."
    }
  },
  "无害标准": {
    "标准1": {
      "内容": "模因不包含任何针对女性的仇恨、偏见或攻击性内容。",
      "对应原文": "A meme is NOT misogynous if it is conceptually not related to women or even if it is related to women, but it does not represent an offensive, sexist or hateful concept against women."
    },
    "标准2": {
      "内容": "模因的内容与女性无关，或仅仅是中立的描述，没有任何贬低或攻击的意图。",
      "对应原文": "A meme that does not express any form of hate against women."
    },
    "标准3": {
      "内容": "模因可能包含幽默或讽刺的元素，但不涉及对女性的贬低或物化。",
      "对应原文": "Although many memes are created with humorous intent, others have political or activist ambitions."
    }
  }
}

### 错误样本ID: 3248

  "判别出错原因分析": "在当前模型对模因的评估中，打分结果明显偏离了Ground Truth（GT），将其误判为无害而实际上是有害。这一错误的主要原因在于对Harmful Scores（有害分数）的判别维度理解不足。首先，在维度H1（Targeted Entity Existence）上，模型未能充分识别该模因间接针对女性的内容。模因文本提到的'THE ONLY GIRL YOU MATCH WITH ON TINDER'，虽然表面上看似在讨论约会，但实际上暗示了对女性在社交交往中受到的物化和羞辱，这种内容属于攻击性和贬低女性的范畴。因此，H1的得分应提升。其次，在维度H2（Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Content）上，内容传达的性别歧视信息未被充分考虑，模型应针对任何对女性有攻击性或贬低性意图的内容给予更高分数。此外，H3（Multimodal Nature of Harm）受图文结合影响严重，其结果未能清晰显现图与文间的有害语境关系。总之，这些维度的得分缺乏对模因整体内容中对女性的潜在贬低的敏感性，这是导致最终错误判别的根本原因。在无害维度N1（No Targeted Entity）上，模型给予了较低评分，但未能充分理解模因的内涵与其可能产生的影响。因此，增加维度以提升现有评估对复杂内容的敏感性，将是必要的改进方向。",

        "details": "此维度主要关注模因文本中是否存在潜在的性别歧视或贬低元素，尽管表面文字可能缺乏直接攻击，但诸如约会平台的引用可能隐含了对女性的物化或假设。评估者应分析文本背后的社会文化语境，判断其是否反映出对女性的不平等期待或评价。此维度的引入将增加对模因复杂性和深层意义的理解，从而提高判别的准确性。"

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因ID: 5718和ID: 3248的错误分析中，专家们提出了一系列关于如何改进模因有害性判别的看法。经过综合分析，我们提出了两条主要的操作建议，以提升对模因中性别歧视内容的敏感性和准确性。

首先，我们建议**新增两个维度**。第一个是“**女性物化的维度（Dimensional Reflection of Objectification）**”，该维度旨在强调模因中女性被物化的现象。当模因描绘女性为物体或满足特定审美标准的存在时，这种情况应当被单独评估。通过引入此维度，可以更全面地评估模因的有害性，特别是在认知女性的社会身份方面。第二个新增的维度是“**幽默内容的背景分析（Contextual Humor Analysis）**”，该维度将单独评估幽默元素对女性的潜在攻击性。这一分析将有助于深入理解幽默是否淡化了性别问题，或是依然带有物化与贬低的意味，从而提升误判的敏感性。

其次，我们将**删除与合并现有维度**。由于模因的性质发生了变化，H1维度（Targeted Entity Existence）表现异常，被判定为漏报，建议删除该维度，以便于合理评估模因对女性的直接攻击意图。而N2维度（Harmless Scores）打分过高，应删除该维度，以清晰反映模因的真正潜在有害性。此外，我们将H和N维度的数量调整至4个，保持整体评估的精简与有效。

最后，在评估打分时，我们特别强调应避免将H得分压制在高分，而N得分则偏低的极端情况。每个维度分数应独立进行，并应充分考虑模因中隐含的性别歧视信息，以保证判别的准确性和公正性。这种改进方案聚焦于提升模因评估模型对复杂社交与文化语境的敏感性，旨在为后续的模因判别过程提供更科学、更具参考价值的依据。


---

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator tasked with scoring a meme based on the MAMI annotation guidelines (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your objective is not to label the meme as 'misogynous' or 'not misogynous,' but to assign scores from 1 to 9 for each dimension, wherein 1 indicates complete absence and 9 denotes full presence.

**Critical Instructions Before Scoring:**

1. **Definition Clarity**  
   - **Harmful Content (Misogynous)**: A meme is deemed harmful if it contains offensive, sexist, or hateful elements directed at women, either implicitly or explicitly.  
   - **Harmless Content (Not Misogynous)**: A meme may be classified as harmless if it does not convey hate against women—either by being unrelated to them or involving them without discriminatory content.

2. **Harm Representation**  
   - Evaluate if harm is presented **implicitly** (e.g., subtle visual cues) or **explicitly** (e.g., direct hate speech). Both forms need to be considered for harmful scoring.

3. **Image-Text Dynamics**  
   - Determine if the offensive meaning arises only through the combination of image and text, both of which must be evaluated together as per MAMI principles.

4. **Contextual Evaluation**  
   - Consider the following queries:
     - "Can this be reasonably interpreted as offensive or hateful toward women?"
     - "Does the meme present negative content about women as a fact or as absurd humor without real-world harm?"
     - "Does it critique gender norms without derogatory framing of women?" If it does, consider it harmless.

**Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria (Misogynous):**
- **H1: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Intent**  
  Score high if the meme targets women with offensive or sexist implications. This encompasses explicit and implicit content aimed at women.

- **H2: Objectification of Women**  
  Score high if the meme depicts women as objects or adheres to specific beauty standards, undermining their social identity.

- **H3: Humor's Contextual Analysis**  
  Score high if the humorous elements are derogatory or imply objectification, which necessitates scrutiny of how humor is positioned within the content.

- **H4: Multimodal Assessment**  
  Score high if harmful perceptions arise from the interplay of image and text working in tandem, as mandated by MAMI's multi-modal framework.

**Harmless Criteria (Not Misogynous):**
- **N1: Absence of Targeted Entity**  
  Score high only if no identifiable woman or female group is depicted in a derogatory manner.

- **N2: Filtering Conditions Adherence**  
  Score high if it meets criteria such as being non-English, unreadable, or merely a single modality (text-only or image-only) without meaningful interaction.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
  Score high if:
    - The content is entirely fantastical without features that represent women negatively, or
    - It critiques societal structures without implicating real women in derogatory contexts. If a real woman is portrayed and labeled derogatorily, assign N3 a score of 3 or below. If depicted in a fictional or fantastical light without such implications, N3 can score 6 or higher.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a concise justification based on MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme includes offensive or sexist elements targeting women (implicit/explicit), (2) whether the harm is dependent on the interaction of image and text, and (3) the rationale for the N3 score based on derogatory content or fantastical context."
}

### 错误样本ID: 8102

  "判别出错原因分析": "此次分数出错的原因主要在于模型未能充分识别出模因中的潜在有害内容。模因的文本部分‘There are two types of women...’暗示了这种分类可能会带有性别歧视的倾向。根据Ground Truth，该模因属于有害（harmful）类别，尽管模型的H1得分为3，表明有一定的有害意图，但没有足够高的分数来反映出其潜在的攻击性或性别歧视。此外，H2的得分为2，这表明模型没有意识到文本可能暗示对女性的物化。虽然图像中的女性面部被遮挡，似乎无意中降低了对女性对象化的指控，但从文本内容来看，仍然可以隐晦地展示出对女性的刻板印象或贬低。这种模因的反映不仅在于具体的视觉元素，也在于文字表达和上下文情境的结合。另一方面，在无害（harmless）维度中，N1得分被评为5，表明模型对女性展示的中立性不够敏感，未能正确识别出文本所带来的潜在针对性。因此，模型总体上尚未达到准确评估模因内容的标准，需要在维度表达和内容分析上进行调整，以更准确地反映模因的有害性，尤其是通过强化H1和H2的评估标准，以对任何暗示性别歧视的情况下进行更严格的分类。",

      "H6": {
        "action": "新增",
        "reason": "引入上下文和语境分析的维度，以应对模因在特定情境中传达的微妙含义。许多模因的攻击性质与其使用的特定语言或视觉元素的构成密切相关，特别是在社交媒体等环境中。这种层次可以帮助更好地理解模因可能产生的影响和后果，而不仅仅是文本或视觉的表层含义。",
        "details": "H6：上下文和语境分析，专注于模因所处的社会、文化、历史背景及其内容的潜在影响。此维度将加强对模因隐含内容的评估，考虑其在实际交流环境中的接受度。例如，通过分析是否有特定文化的语境可以解释模因中的幽默或攻击性，或者是否该模因在某个社区中具有负面影响。然而，忽略这些因素可能导致对模因整体含义的误解。"
      }
    }
  }
}
